2025-02-05 13:27:07,461 - WARNING - Attempting fallback parsing on: To solve this problem, we need to determine whether most events occurred in the United States based on given data. The solution involves counting the number of events that took place in the U.S. and comparing it with the total number of events that have location information.

### Approach
1. **Extract Location Data**: Iterate through each event to check if a location is specified.
2. **Count U.S. Events**: For events that specify a location, count how many were held in the United States.
3. **Compare Counts**: Determine if the number of events in the U.S. is more than half of all events with location data.

### Solution Code
```python
def most_events_in_us(events):
    us_count = 0
    total_location_events = 0
    for event in events:
        # Check if 'location' is present and not empty
        if 'location' in event and event['location']:
            total_location_events += 1
            if event['location'] == 'United States':
                us_count += 1
    # Determine if U.S. events are the majority
    return us_count > (total_location_events / 2)
```

### Explanation
- **Extract Location Data**: The code checks each event to see if it contains a location. If it does, and that location is 'United States', it increments the count of U.S. events.
- **Count Comparison**: After counting all relevant events, the function checks whether the number of U.S. events exceeds half of the total events with location data. This comparison determines if most events occurred in the U.S.

This approach ensures that we accurately count and compare only the relevant events, providing a clear answer based on majority.
